[Mr. Sakai Toshihiko Suddenly Goes Insane] 48

Tokyo Dispatch from Japan United News Agency on the 17th: Sakai Toshihiko, a veteran of the Japanese socialist movement, is 63 years old. Last year, he suddenly collapsed near his home due to a cerebral hemorrhage. He has since been recuperating at home, but his condition recently took a turn for the worse, and he began to show signs of mental derangement. As a result of discussions between his family and friends, he was sent to Aoyama Mental Hospital for treatment. The cause of Mr. Sakai's madness is quite complex. The hospital has prohibited all visits.

American Veterans Demonstrate Before Congress Adjourns

Demanding the Issuance of Remaining Bonus Payments

Washington Dispatch from the National News Agency on the 16th: The U.S. Congress adjourned at 11:30 PM tonight. As today's Congress was in session, veteran representatives, aware of the imminent adjournment, again gathered 15,000 people on the Capitol lawn to petition, chanting slogans and demanding that Congress resolve to immediately provide cash loans for the remaining $2.24 billion in veterans' bonus certificates for relief. However, Congress ultimately found it difficult to agree due to the strained state of the national treasury. After several discussions, they had managed to balance the budget. Where could they find such a huge sum? Therefore, Vice President Curtis ordered the police to disperse the crowd on the grounds that their clamor outside was disrupting national proceedings. The veteran representatives resisted the order. The police were then summoned to drive them away and arrest their leader, Waters. However, the veterans remained steadfastly unwilling to disperse. They dispatched a representative, Everett, to the White House to petition the President, but the President refused to see him. Upon hearing this news, over a hundred veterans went to demonstrate in front of the White House but were dispersed by the police. As for the 10,000 people in front of Congress, they persisted for a long time. Upon hearing that Congress had adjourned and seeing that all hope was lost, they finally formed ranks and departed.

British Government Invites Germany to Join Political Consultation Agreement

Berlin Dispatch from the National News Agency on the 16th: The British government has invited Germany to join the pan-European political consultation agreement, based on the Franco-British accord signed in Lausanne. According to a semi-official statement issued today, European countries had already exchanged such ideals in Lausanne, and the German government had expressed sympathy at the time and still holds this attitude. However, since the German government was not initially involved in these negotiations, it must first investigate the relationship of the agreement before accepting the British government's invitation.

Anglo-Irish Negotiations Fail

De Valera Hurries Back to Dublin

British Government Issues Statement

Proposing Two Arbitration Methods

Dublin Dispatch from Havas on the 16th: When de Valera's ship arrived in port, a large crowd stood on the shore to watch. Although Mr. de Valera was very tired, he still had a beaming smile. The welcomers madly shouted "No surrender! Long live de Valera!" Most of the cabinet members were at the port to greet him. After disembarking, Mr. de Valera refused to make any statements to reporters and immediately drove back to his office to report the results of the London negotiations to government officials. Before boarding the ship in Holyhead to return to Ireland, Mr. de Valera had a telephone conversation with London, reportedly with British financial authorities, to discuss the issuance of a public statement. According to opinions in Irish political circles, it is still uncertain when the Anglo-Irish negotiations will resume.

London Dispatch from Havas on the 16th: After de Valera met with the British Prime Minister in London, someone asked Labour leader Ramsay MacDonald for his opinion on the failure of the recent Anglo-Irish negotiations. Mr. MacDonald replied that he believed the failure of these negotiations constituted a blemish on civilization. Mr. MacDonald also said, "I very much hope that the Pope and the Archbishop of Canterbury can, in the name of the Church, mediate between the British and Irish governments, so that they can implement the spirit of forgiveness preached by the founder of Christianity in resolving this dispute."

London Dispatch from Reuters on the 16th: Official sources report that the British government has proposed to de Valera, Chairman of the Executive Council of the Free State, that if they can agree on the terms of arbitration for the Anglo-Irish disputes or continue discussions and pay the outstanding debts, then the British government may temporarily suspend the special tariffs on goods from the Free State.

London Dispatch from Reuters on the 16th: Tonight, the British government issued an important statement regarding the Irish dispute, stating that on June 10, the British government formally suggested to de Valera that the land annuity dispute be submitted to arbitration. The Free State government then raised various difficulties regarding how the arbitration tribunal should be organized. Although they were unwilling to engage in close negotiations with London on this matter, they ultimately proposed to the British government that the Free State government and the British government each appoint two commissioners to jointly investigate the facts. However, they did not mention that both sides should abide by the decisions of the commission, only stating that the two governments should engage in negotiations when the four commissioners draft a report. No method was proposed to reach a compromise agreement if negotiations failed. The British government now proposes: (1)

Page 8

Since this dispute involves money, it should be adjudicated by a court. Before a ruling is made, land annuities should continue to be paid as usual. (2) Once the terms for arbitration or continued negotiations and the method of payment have been agreed upon, all current actions, including the imposition of special tariffs, will be suspended. The British government intends to negotiate this agreement as soon as it receives a reply from the Irish Free State in order to end the dispute.

French Parliament Passes Bill to Issue Bonds

Totaling 20 Billion Francs

To Cover Budget Deficit

Paris Dispatch from Reuters on the 16th: The French Senate and National Assembly have passed a proposal to issue 20 billion francs in treasury bonds to cover the budget deficit. When Premier Édouard Herriot took office after the French elections, he knew that the budget deficit was 5 billion francs. Therefore, Herriot's finance minister submitted a bill to the National Assembly stipulating a reduction in expenditures of 2.5 billion francs and an increase in taxes, which was expected to increase revenue by 1.5 billion francs. It was estimated that there would still be a shortfall of 1 billion francs, so it was necessary to issue new bonds to make up the difference. The largest reduction in French expenditures was in military spending, with a total reduction of 1.5 billion francs from the army, navy, and air force budgets. As for civil servants, salaries were reduced across the board, starting from the President and cabinet ministers.

U.S. Trade Deficit Last Month

Cash Continues to Flow Out

Washington Dispatch from Reuters on the 16th: The U.S. Department of Commerce released a trade report stating that U.S. imports exceeded exports in June, marking the first trade deficit this year. In June, U.S. imports were valued at $121 million, while exports were valued at $115 million. For the past six months of this year, U.S. foreign trade has still been in surplus, but it has fallen from $208,816,000 in the first half of 1931 to $84,249,000, a decrease of $164,567,000. U.S. cash continued to flow out in June. Gold exports were valued at $226 million, while gold imports were valued at only $18 million, resulting in a net loss of $208 million. In the same month last year, gold exports were valued at $40,000 and imports were valued at $64 million.

German Poet's 70th Birthday

Hindenburg Presents Medal

Berlin Dispatch from the National News Agency on the 14th: Today is the 70th birthday of Germany's famous poet and playwright, Fulda. German President Hindenburg sent a congratulatory telegram and presented the Goethe Medal for Science and Art to mark the occasion.

Important News

Far East War Can Resolve World Panic

Osaka Asahi Shimbun reports that when former Ambassador to France, Yoshizawa, returned to his country, a high-ranking official of a French arms company, named Roche, went to the Paris train station to see him off and discussed the supply of military supplies for the Far East war. Since the European war, most of the arms manufacturing factories in Europe and the United States have been shut down. Now, in view of the changing situation in the Far East, all famous arms factories and chemical companies in Europe are busy rushing to manufacture weapons in preparation for supplying the war in the East. On one hand, they are newly hiring laborers and renewing the organization of factories, and some factories even openly hoist the banner of "Manufacturing for the Far East War" high above their chimneys, fluttering in the sky. It is reported that France has already imported 800 million francs of military supplies to Japan, and this amount is still on the books. They are all products of the French Schneider arms factory. Other countries such as Germany and the United States have also exported large quantities of arms to the East, so the stock prices of military equipment in various countries are gradually rising. It can be said to be prosperity in the midst of depression. Moreover, in terms of the intentions of various countries, they also very much hope for the outbreak of the Far East war. Many of their arguments say that "war can resolve world panic," for example: (1) The German Mining News argues that the outbreak of war will inevitably affect the prices of military industry and various mineral products. According to reports in Paris, the Far East war seems to have a positive impact on opening up the world panic. (2) Norway's Oslo Morning Post claims that the Far East war is difficult to avoid. In other words, although war is a cruel act, in order to seek world prosperity, it is deeply hoped that this war will be created. After all, the demand for ships will inevitably increase with the outbreak of war, promoting speculation in rising prices. (3) Denmark's Financier Post claims that a single move in the Far East war can save the current panic and remove Denmark's exchange restriction order. If the war spreads to the entire Asian war, it can raise the standard of world prices, and world production can also recover from the dead end. Therefore, in order to get out of this deep depression, we have to expect this unexpected event. (4) American economic observer Babson said, "If Japan declares war on Russia, then we can expect the recovery of the world economic situation, and the killing tools stored by various countries due to the Far East war can be sold well, and a large number of unemployed people in various countries can also be hired to manufacture military supplies."

Ma Zhanshan's Troops Engage the Enemy at Dahuangtai

The Two Armies Are Still Facing Each Other Between Bayan and Mulan

The Jilin Self-Defense Army Is Actively Moving Towards the Provincial Capital

Harbin Correspondence: Xu Baozhen's brigade stationed in Nehe County, Heilongjiang Province, was originally the guard regiment of the Heilongjiang Border Defense Commander's Office before the Nenjiang battle. In the battle of Tao'ang Road, Ma Zhanshan personally led this unit to annihilate Japanese soldiers in Daxing and Sanjianfang. The soldiers were loyal and brave, and were the crown of the Heilongjiang army. When Ma Zhanshan feigned surrender, he was incorporated into the 3rd Infantry Brigade and stationed in Nehe, serving as a shield for the Heihe area in advance. After Ma's departure, Xu was secretly instructed to wait for an opportunity to move. When the troops on the Huhu and Qike roads were fiercely fighting, Xu led his troops to respond, but before he could act, the Japanese Army's Amano Brigade was stationed in the county to monitor him. Therefore, Xu's brigade did not dare to move lightly. Recently, Ma led his troops to fight in the lower reaches of the Songhua River and in the eastern part of Heilongjiang. The Japanese army then concentrated on the Nenjiang-Qike road. The Koizumi Regiment of the Hiramatsu Brigade entered Nehe, intending to take the opportunity to resolve Xu's brigade. On July 8, Koizumi falsely claimed to hold a banquet, held a banquet in the Business Association, and invited Xu to drink. Xu had heard about it in advance, so on one hand, he excused himself due to illness, and on the other hand, he concentrated the main force of his troops that night, drove out of the city, and stationed his troops on the Gan River of Nehe. The cavalry company launched a fierce attack on the Japanese barracks at night. Because the Japanese army had already been prepared, they withdrew after a short battle. On the morning of the 9th, the two sides fought fiercely inside and outside the city. The Japanese army relied on the high and thick city walls, erected field artillery and fired, and the regimental commander Koizumi led cavalry and artillery soldiers out of the city, trying to cross the river and attack from both sides. Xu's brigade had already placed artillery in the area. When the Japanese army was halfway across the river, they opened fire and bombarded them, killing dozens of Japanese soldiers in the water. The remnants retreated to the city and held on, while sending a telegram to ask for help. On the morning of the 10th, the Japanese army brigade at the Ningnian station on the Qike road heard the news and rushed to help. That night, Xu's brigade met them on the river bank. The Japanese army had several times the advantage and pressed hard. Xu's brigade was unable to resist and retreated to the vicinity of Nenjiang, where they joined forces with Xu Zihe's cavalry and more than 4,000 militiamen who had just arrived from Heihe. Their momentum was huge. They had abandoned Nehe Nenjiang and advanced along the Qike road towards the capital of Heilongjiang Province. Most of the Japanese troops on the Qike line had been transferred back to Longsha and set up defenses in the four suburbs. Deng Wen's brigade of the Heilongjiang army, about 2,000 people, together with thousands of the Big Sword Society and Red Spear Society, began to attack Keshan from Baiquan on the 9th. The Japanese army, led by the main force of the Hiramatsu Brigade, guarded Keshan County and Longgou on the Qike road. The two armies opened fire at noon on the 9th. Deng's brigade mainly attacked the county seat, and the Red Spear Society and Big Sword Society attacked Longgou. In the evening, Deng's brigade, which attacked the city, had charged to Cuijia Inn, three miles away from the city. The Japanese army resisted desperately, relying on the sweeping power of their light and heavy machine guns. Deng's brigade had to retreat. After 7 p.m., they retreated to the northeast of Keshan. This force was arranged by Ma Zhanshan in this area, specifically to contain the Japanese army on the Qike road, so their retreat was not far away. The Japanese army dared not move far away from the traffic routes because they were afraid of the heat and mosquitoes. The two sides were still facing each other remotely. The battalion commanded by Ma Zhanshan himself had been retreating towards the east of Heilongjiang along the river between Bayan Mulan, Tonghe, and Tanghuyuan since the 7th, trying to draw the Japanese army away from the railway line and encircle them. The Japanese army planned to encircle them with the entire force of the Hiraga Brigade and the 6th Division and destroy the Heilongjiang army in one fell swoop between Qingcheng and Wangkui. In order to break the Japanese army's plan, Ma used the troops of Cai Hongyou and Li Tiande to harass various places on the Huhu road Xinglongzhen, Sihuantai in Suihua, and Zhaoxingzhen in Hailun, enticing the enemy in various ways. The movements of the various units were unpredictable. Xinglongzhen was once destroyed by Li Tiande's army on the evening of the 9th, and traffic was cut off. A small team of Japanese troops was annihilated and more than 40 Japanese soldiers were killed. There have also been battles in Beixingzhen recently. It is rumored that the Japanese army is at a disadvantage and reinforcements and planes have been sent from Hailun to rescue them. The details are still not very clear here. The Japanese army, wanting to defeat the main force of the Heilongjiang army, desperately pursued Ma Zhanshan's eastward march. Their battalions of cavalry and infantry moved forward in several branches, checking and responding to each other. Ma Zhanshan, fearing attacks by Japanese planes and avoiding marching in the summer heat, moved at night and, due to his familiarity with the geography, repeatedly caused the Japanese army to lose track of him. On July 9, Ma's battalion arrived at the Dahuangtai area near Bayan County and was caught up by the Hiraga Brigade of the Japanese army. They opened fire at 7 a.m. that day. The Japanese army used mountain guns and heavy artillery to attack from both sides, and four planes dropped bombs. Ma Zhanshan ordered the cavalry and infantry to divide and resist the enemy. At 10 a.m., the battle was at its fiercest. A plane, flying at low altitude, used machine guns to sweep downwards and was hit by a mortar from the Heilongjiang army. It caught fire in the air and fell behind the Japanese army's position. The other planes then stopped shooting at low altitude. Around 3 p.m., 700 cavalrymen from Cai Hongyou's brigade came to join the battle from the Huhu line, attacking from the rear. The Japanese army's position was thrown into chaos. Ma led his troops to take the opportunity to launch a fierce attack. The Japanese army suffered countless deaths and fled in panic towards Jiangjiadian. The Heilongjiang army then retreated calmly to Bayan. On the morning of the 10th, the troops of the Japanese Hitoe Branch rode Jianglun ships down the Songhua River to Wuhe. After landing, they wanted to respond to the Hiraga unit and attack Bayan from both sides. This was discovered by the Heilongjiang army. After the army landed, they were surrounded on the river bank and subjected to a frontal attack, killing about 300 enemies. Many were drowned in the river. That day, river navigation was cut off, and ships upstream and downstream could not pass. The remnants of the Hitoe branch were besieged for a day and night. On the morning of the 11th, 2,000 Japanese troops and a brigade of puppet Jilin troops were dispatched from Harbin, with the coordination of five planes, to rescue the remnants. Currently, the two armies are facing each other between Bayan and Mulan. The Japanese army continues to concentrate its forces there. Ma Zhanshan also dispatched the Tonghe and Tangyuan militia to support. A Japanese regiment in Yilan was originally going to return and sail up the river to attack the Heilongjiang army by water. However, on the evening of the 10th, because the soldiers were arguing with the puppet Jilin army in a brothel, 60 people were ambushed and killed by Liu Shu's 7th Brigade of the puppet Jilin army. The puppet Jilin army, fearing disaster, specially invited Li Du's army to attack, willing to be internal responders. Li's army, led by Lu Yongcai, had arrived 30 miles south of Yilan and had a fierce battle with the Japanese army. Although Liu Shu's brigade did not respond, they sat and watched, so the Japanese army could not move to support the Bayan area. As for the main cavalry force of Gong Changhai's army of the Jilin Self-Defense Army, it has arrived at Tumenling on the Jilin-Changchun road and is moving towards the provincial capital. A plainclothes team mixed into Changchun on the evening of the 9th and set fire to destroy two Japanese aircraft hangars. (July 11)

Twenty Regiments of Troops Have Been Dispatched in Recent Days

Bandit Activity Reported Again in Lianping and Heping in Eastern Guangdong

Guangzhou Communication: The fierce fighting between troops and bandits in northern Guangdong is intensifying. The 1st Army and 2nd Division are holding Ganzhou, the 1st Division is holding Dageng, the 4th Division is in Xinfeng, and other areas and transportation routes are occupied by bandits. Zhu Mao Peng's Various Bands Fleeing to Northern Guangdong

The Bandit Troops Are Advancing into Guangdong in Three Routes

Five Provinces Mobilize to Encircle and Suppress the Bandits

Nanchang Communication: Zhu Mao Peng Li and other major bands, threatened by the Fujian and Hunan armies, advanced east along the Jiangxi-Hunan border and west along the Jiangxi-Fujian border, converging in Xinfeng Xunwu on the Jiangxi-Guangdong border. Bandit leaders, such as Xiang Ying, chairman of the false Military Commission, Zhu De and Ji Zhendong, commanders of the 1st and 2nd Group Armies, and above the false army commander, attended the meeting. It was decided to take advantage of the internal strife between the two Chens, the sparsity of the Guangdong-Jiangxi defense army, concentrate the bandit masses, and disturb Guangdong in three routes. After all, Guangdong is an area of wealth, and there are many civilian guns. If they break through Nanxiong Dageng and other places, they can seize a large number of guns, bullets, oil, salt, rice, cloth, etc., to compensate for the losses in Fujian. It was also predetermined that if they win, they will occupy Shaoguan and integrate the bandits in northern Guangdong, western Fujian, southern Jiangxi, and eastern Hunan. Peng's bandits used this as a base after failing to attack Ganzhou last year, designating Chongyi Yougui and other counties as the false Xiangjiangxi Province, with Yingqian as the provincial capital. Various false agencies were set up here, serving as the general agency for redifying southeastern Hunan and western Jiangxi. An unknown number of bandits were killed. The corpses were scattered all over Yingqian. There were no traces of bandits. Misunderstanding Suddenly Arises Among Troops Stationed in Xuzhou

Page 11

Local News: Northwestern Aviation Route Actively Being Prepared. If the Fuel Problem Along the Way Can Be Solved, Full Operation Expected Within the Year. The Northwestern air route, actively being prepared by the Eurasia Aviation Corporation, has already opened this year, with a section from Beijing to Lanzhou. Currently, preparations are underway for the entire length of the route, and it is expected that full operation will be possible within the year. A reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency interviewed Mr. Wang Zhiyuan, the manager of the company, and Mr. Xu Mutang, the secretary, yesterday to inquire about the equipment for the Eurasia air route. They provided a very detailed response, which is recorded as follows:

Motivation for Preparation

The preparation for the Northwestern air route was originally part of the company's plan. The company began preparations as soon as it was established. As a result, last year, it opened a route from Shanghai to Berlin, Germany. However, the route was quite circuitous, requiring travel from Shanghai to Ping, then north across Manchuria to Manzhouli, where German planes would take over to fly to Berlin. This route passed through Moscow, Irkutsk, and other places within Russian territory. Therefore, Russian trains were used for transportation from Manzhouli to Moscow. Only in Moscow were German planes used for the connecting flight. Consequently, there were significant delays along the way. Although it was much faster than boats or vehicles, the journey from Shanghai to Berlin still took seven or eight days.

Recent Decision

Last year, the Eurasia aircraft on our side mistakenly flew into Outer Mongolian territory and were forced to be detained, causing the Northwest route to be interrupted. After the September 18th Incident, the Northeast fell, and the recovery of Northwest aviation became hopeless. Therefore, the company sought other solutions. Mr. Li Jingcong, the former director of the transportation business group, went to Ping to prepare the "Hu Xin" route, meaning the route from Shanghai to Xinjiang. The route would pass through Shanghai to Nanjing, to Beiping, and then west to Dihua, which would be the midpoint. However, the company felt that this route was still too circuitous and inconvenient. So, they changed their strategy to make it a direct line from Shanghai to Dihua. Although there would still be some detours, it would not be a large detour. This is the company's most recent decision.

Trunk and Branch Lines

The current Northwest route takes the Shanghai-Xinjiang (Shanghai to Dihua) route as the trunk line and the Beijing-Ping line as the branch line. According to the original decision, the stops along the way include Shanghai, Nanjing, Hankou, Luoyang, Guanyintang, Tongguan, Xi'an, Lanzhou, Xining, Hami, and Dihua. Currently, the trunk line only runs from Nanjing to Luoyang, and the branch line runs from Nanjing to Beiping. For the trunk line, there are plans to first extend it to Lanzhou and then to Dihua.

Fuel Problem

Mr. Wang Zhiyuan went to inspect the Northwest route in June and has now returned to Shanghai. He reported that the Northwest area has many high mountains and steep ridges, so the equipment for flying must be very reliable. The most difficult problem currently is the fuel issue. Because the area is mostly wilderness, there are no gas stations along the way. Once fuel is depleted, flight is impossible. The current plan is to transport fuel from Outer Mongolia using camels, as the area is mostly desert, and there is no other suitable means of transportation besides camels.

Date of Opening

The exact date for the opening of the Northwest air route has not yet been determined. However, if the company can proceed actively and the fuel equipment can be fully resolved, then a date for operation can be set. If progress is rapid, it should be possible to realize this by the end of this year. In the future, travel from Shanghai to Xinjiang will only take three days. Also, after this route is established, air travel between China and Germany can be connected from Dihua with German planes, directly linking to Berlin.

Wu Song Forts Closed to Visitors

The Wusong Fortress, originally a crucial gateway for national defense, has always been closed to visitors. Although the interior of the forts has been destroyed by warfare, the surrounding terrain has not changed. Now, the gateway is open, allowing anyone to visit. Moreover, foreigners often go there to take photos at will. If this is not prohibited, the terrain of the forts will be clear to everyone, not only revealing the weaknesses of the country but also greatly affecting reconstruction. Li Jingye, the Seventh District Chief of the Wusong Public Security Bureau, has received instructions from above to prohibit visits. He notified the Seventh Security Platoon stationed at the fort yesterday that, effective immediately, all people, both Chinese and foreign, are prohibited from visiting.

Deadly Epidemic: Death Within Minutes

Victim Was Wang Zaitang

Fear of Infection from Eating Yumberries

Recently, the weather has been extremely hot, especially in the afternoons. The asphalt on the ground melts and softens, making it easy for people walking on the streets to contract the epidemic. Once contracted, it develops rapidly and is incurable, with some people dying within hours or even minutes. It is horrifying to hear. One afternoon at 1 PM, a man, Mr. Jia, around 50 years old and resembling a laborer, was carrying a basket containing two bowls each of cooked vegetarian dishes, including soybeans and eggplant. He intended to deliver them somewhere. While passing the Ningfu Lane entrance on Glock Road in the French Concession, he felt the epidemic and could not walk. He sat on the roadside and experienced diarrhea. Within ten minutes, he collapsed and died. A policeman reported the incident to the police station, which transported the body to the Tongren Fuyuan branch morgue for examination. As there were no family members, the Second Special Court was notified the next morning. Wu Xiaoke, a prosecutor, and a forensic doctor went to the morgue to examine the body and determined that the deceased had died from illness. The body was handed over to Tongren Fuyuan Hall for burial. As the deceased died from the epidemic and the weather was hot, the body could not be kept for long. Therefore, photos were taken, and the body was immediately placed in a coffin and transported to the cemetery in Pudong for burial. It was not until yesterday afternoon that the deceased's sister, Zhao Wang, arrived at the hall and identified the deceased as Wang Zaitang, 51 years old, from Suzhou. She said that he had always been healthy and likely died from eating yumberries and contracting the epidemic. It can be seen that during this hot weather, food on the stalls is covered with flies. Buyers who are not careful and purchase such food are likely to cause a major life-threatening disaster and should be cautious.

A Couple Commits Suicide in the Bund Park

Embracing and Kissing at Night

Mandarin Ducks Die Together in the Waves

During the summer, the weather is hot, and public and private gardens have become popular places to cool off. There is a park on the south bank of the Huangpu River estuary, in the Shanghai area, which was established by the Shanghai Municipal Council of the Public Concession. Although not very large, it has green trees that provide shade. Visitors feel cool and refreshed because it faces the Huangpu River, and a gentle breeze blows from the river. Therefore, the park has been very popular recently, especially in the evening when the sun sets and the lights come on. People take advantage of their leisure time after dinner to come to the park to cool off. Modern men and women consider the park a good place to talk privately. They stroll hand in hand into the evening, and it is crowded even at midnight. Yesterday at 2:10 AM, a young man and woman were sitting side by side on a bench on the beach in the park. They were both dressed in modern attire. It was late at night, and there were very few visitors in the park. This couple was noticed by a Westerner sitting a short distance away. Although the Westerner could not hear what the two were saying and could not understand Chinese, their actions were very clear. He saw the two embrace and kiss for a long time, then suddenly walk hand in hand to the beach and jump into the river to commit suicide. Only splashes of water were seen, and their traces disappeared. The Westerner wanted to help but was too late. He waited until 3:25 AM when a Chinese patrolman, No. 45, from the Lujiazui Customs Water Patrol Station came by boat from a distance. The Westerner told him what he had seen in detail. The patrolman returned to the police station to report and record the incident for investigation. Although the young couple were buried in the river, their names, ages, and reasons for suicide are still unknown.

Dafeng Factory Workers Staged a Slowdown Yesterday

To Support Unemployed and Arrested Workers

Du Ruoqiu and Others Have Been Transferred to the Court

According to Dagong News Agency, more than 100 unemployed workers from the Dafeng Dyeing and Weaving Factory on Guangfu Road in western Shanghai requested to return to work, resulting in a conflict with the police. Fifteen workers, including Du Ruoqiu, were arrested by the Sixth District Public Security Bureau. It has been learned that the arrested workers have been transferred to the court for interrogation. All the employed workers staged a slowdown yesterday, and the Third District Dyeing Industry Union has submitted a petition to the Party and government agencies for assistance. The details are recorded as follows:

Arrested Persons Sent to Court

The fifteen unemployed workers from the Dafeng Factory, including Du Ruoqiu, Cao Guisen, Huang Yugen, Dui Fuxin, Ye Yukuan, Jin Meilin, and Huang Guifang, were arrested by the Sixth District Police Station and then transferred to the Third Section of the Municipal Public Security Bureau. After a brief interrogation, the Third Section, considering that the case involved assaulting police officers, transferred them to the court for trial on the afternoon of the 16th with a written report.

Employed Workers Staged Slowdown to Help

The factory originally had more than 400 workers. After the January 28th Incident, due to the decline in business, 108 workers were laid off. The remaining 300 workers continued to work in the factory. After the arrest of the 15 unemployed workers, all the employed workers were outraged and stopped working, demanding that the factory accept the unemployed workers' request to return to work. However, the factory did not accept the request, and the employed workers staged a slowdown to help. Yesterday, except for a small number of female workers (who were not members of the union and still went to work), all the male workers, more than 300, refused to work.

Union Reported to the Party and Government

The petition stated: "We are submitting this petition regarding the labor-management dispute at the Dafeng Factory. The matter has been reported previously, and we have recently been informed that personnel have been dispatched to investigate. Unexpectedly, the factory used the Sixth District Police Station to send a large number of armed police officers, led by Lu Shiyi, the personnel director of the factory, to the union hall, where they arrested worker Du Ruoqiu without cause. When they encountered Huang Guifang, a director and secretary of the union, they arrested him as well. When the workers saw this, they gathered in front of the district gate to demand the release of union director Huang Guifang and member Du Ruoqiu, maintaining order and without any disturbances. However, the police arbitrarily arrested the unarmed workers and physically assaulted them, even using box cannons to beat them until they were covered in injuries, arresting more than a dozen people. We do not know what laws the police district is relying on to interfere in the labor-management disputes of the union, and the innocent workers have suffered such pain. Under the Party's rule, how can such illegal actions be tolerated? Therefore, we implore your union (bureau) to uphold justice and handle the matter fairly, bring the perpetrators to justice, and advise the Public Security Bureau to release the innocent immediately, so as to deter others and ensure future stability. It is for the public good. We submit this to the Municipal Party Committee and the Bureau of Social Affairs, the Third District Dyeing Industry Union of Shanghai." It is also heard that the union has scheduled an emergency meeting today to discuss countermeasures.

An elderly man from Jiading, Lu Songquan, around 60 years old, wearing a gray cloth gown, was walking slowly and could not avoid the bus in time. He was knocked to the ground and suffered head injuries. Police officer No. 1212 from the Xinzha Police Station arrived at the scene, recorded the driver's information, and sent the injured man to Renji Hospital for treatment. Unfortunately, the injuries were too severe, and he died upon arrival at the hospital. His body was sent to the morgue for examination.

Girl Falls into Ice Cellar and Freezes to Death

The second daughter of Li Yusheng, the owner of the Tiansheng Tang Pharmacy on the Six Mile Bridge Main Street in Pudong, was only 10 years old. Yesterday at 9 AM, she went to play alone at a nearby ice factory. No one noticed at the time, and the girl went deep into the ice piles. Due to the slippery ice surface, she accidentally fell into the ice cellar. By the time she was discovered and rescued, she had already frozen to death. The factory sent someone to notify the deceased's family to prepare a coffin and collect the body.

Notorious Bandit Yang Guirong, Who Opened Fire and Refused Arrest, Executed by Shooting

The notorious bandit Yang Guirong, who repeatedly colluded with accomplices to rob villagers of their property and shoot the victims in the Songhu area, and Li Xingge, were encountered by officers of the Second Team of the Shanghai Provincial Water Police in Longwang Temple in Pudong. When the officers approached to arrest them, the bandits opened fire and refused arrest, leading to a fierce battle lasting several hours. Li Xingge was shot and injured on the spot. He tried to escape by swimming but drowned due to his injuries. His body floated to the 66th Tu area of the 19th Bao in Jinshan County. The Bao reported the incident to the county for verification and burial. At the same time, the bandit Yang Guirong was captured and sent to the District Department for interrogation. He confessed to colluding with others to rob and resisting arrest. He was immediately transferred to the Garrison Headquarters, which reviewed the evidence and found it to be conclusive. He was sentenced to death in accordance with the regulations for punishing bandits and was executed by shooting in Shanghai the day before yesterday.

Swiss National Gu Qi Accused of Illicit Arms Trafficking

The Shanghai Times reported that Swiss national Gu Qi was arrested by Western Detective Harvey of the Huishi Police Station on Friday night, accused of illicit arms trafficking. He was taken to the Swiss Consulate General for interrogation on the morning of the 16th and detained for further investigation. Harvey and a Chinese detective received a tip and went to Yinghua Street near the Datong Dance Hall, where they encountered Gu Qi. The Chinese detective pretended to be a representative of a buyer and asked if he had any arms for sale. Gu Qi invited him to a nearby secret room and showed him four pistols and some ammunition. The detective pretended to agree on a price and then pretended to report to his boss, informing Harvey. Gu Qi was arrested with the evidence.

Lu Ziqing Sues Wife for Cohabitation

Wife Says She Was Never Formally Married

Debate Concluded Yesterday, Awaiting Judgment

Lu Ziqing, a native of Funing, recently sued his wife, Ji Fengqing, for refusing to return home and living with her mother. He believed that his mother-in-law, Ji Tao, and his brother-in-law, Ji Xiuquan, had instigated her actions. He hired a lawyer to file a lawsuit in the First Special Court, requesting cohabitation. His argument was that he had married Ji Fengqing as his second wife ten years ago. They were initially harmonious and had a son and a daughter. However, in recent years, she was seduced by her mother and brother and dared to run away with her children in February of this year. Fortunately, he found her after searching everywhere, but after returning home and cohabitating for only a few days, she repeated her actions on April 2, taking all her belongings and her children while he was away. A neighbor surnamed Deng witnessed her brother, Ji Xiuquan, and others helping her hire a car and move away. While he was investigating, she preemptively filed a false accusation against him with the Shanghai Local Court Procuratorate, claiming that he had abandoned her. The court issued a summons, and after a hearing, ordered them to cohabitate. However, after leaving the court, she was forcibly taken away by her mother and brother, preventing him from cohabitating with his wife and seeing his children. He was very angry and had attempted mediation, but it failed. Therefore, he filed a lawsuit, requesting that Ji Fengqing and her children be ordered to return home. The trial was held yesterday by Judge Qiao Wanxuan. Ji Fengqing hired lawyer Zhang Ding to represent her, while Ji Tao and Ji Xiuquan hired lawyer Fan Gang to defend them. Lu Ziqing first presented his case, requesting that Ji Fengqing be ordered to cohabitate. However, Ji Fengqing argued that she and Lu Ziqing were not husband and wife but were in a concubinage relationship. When she first met Lu, he falsely claimed that he had no wife. Later, she discovered that he already had a wife, but she could not undo the situation because they had children. Recently, he hid the children she had given birth to in Room 6 of the Nanyang Hotel in Xieqiao, intending to sell them. She discovered this and reported it to the police, who rescued the children. Moreover, he has no formal occupation and spends his days with hooligans, neglecting her livelihood. Given his malicious intentions, she could not possibly cohabitate with him and therefore refused to return home. Subsequently, lawyer Fan spoke on behalf of his clients, completely denying Lu's claims. Judge Qiao then declared the debate closed and adjourned the court to await a scheduled judgment.

Hongkou Organizations Petition the Municipal Government to Revise Rent Exemption Measures

More than 20 organizations, including the Hongkou District Branches of the Citizens' Federation and the United Associations of Business Circles of Tangshan Road, Dongyouheng Road, Chuzhou Road, Yichuan Road, Yangshupu Road, Zhoujiazui Road, Broadway Road, East and West Huade Road, Yinxiang Road, Haining Road, Boundary Road, Kunnenghai Road, North Xizang Road, Chuanbao Road, Suzhou Road, North Shanxi Road, North Jiangxi Road, and Wuchang Road, resolved at the Sixteenth Representative Conference that the Hongkou area suffered from the atrocities of the Japanese army during the Songhu War, resulting in a strike lasting more than 60 days and causing significant losses. The rent exemption issued by the Municipal Government does not reflect the facts or human sentiment and is unfair. They requested the Municipal Government to revise it. The petition to the Municipal Government is attached below: The petition is regarding the issuance of rent exemption, which does not reflect the facts and is unfair. We implore you to revise the measures to address public opinion. We, the associations in the Hongkou area, have always been occupied by the Japanese. During the January 28th Incident, the defense committees of various countries were unable to intervene, and the area north of the Suzhou River was entirely controlled by the Japanese army, who carried out atrocities, slaughtering and raping at will, even using places like the Sanyuan Palace as killing machines. How could the people not flee? South of the Suzhou River, the 41st Army painfully opened the market, but the Hongkou area was in a state of terror and dared not rashly open the market, continuing the strike for more than a month, resulting in even greater losses. Since the advocacy of rent exemption, enlightened landlords, such as the Continental Bank, Shanghai Bank, Pacific Foreign Firm, and Dehe Foreign Firm, have been willing to exempt rent for three months. However, the issued notice on rent exemption grants up to two and a half months north of the Suzhou River. The following two points should be opposed: first, the municipal authorities have not weighed the facts and human sentiments and have issued inaccurate points. Second, how should the three months of rent that have already been exempted be handled, which has caused disputes. For the sake of resolving disputes among citizens, we urgently seek the issuance of rent exemption measures to alleviate the pain. Unexpectedly, the result is the opposite, greatly disappointing the people and causing public opinion to be in an uproar. Looking at the market after the disaster, it is extremely difficult. A three-month rent exemption in the Hongkou area north of the Suzhou River is not enough to demonstrate fairness. In order to eliminate market disputes and achieve peace, we have no choice but to appeal to your government to promptly withdraw the order and reissue measures to appease public opinion and alleviate the difficulties of businesses. We are deeply grateful and eagerly await your command.

Sha Tian Property Owners Given Deadline to Pay Price Increase

The Shanghai County Government Shangbao Shatien Official Property Bureau issued a notice yesterday stating that official Hamadi land and the original new beach fields as well as the non-food overflow lands, all belong to the scope of Shatien's official property, which are all national properties. It is not permitted by law, regardless of the duration of occupation. Should there be those who happen to be hiding the occupation without reporting, then, not only will they be violating the provisions, but they will be abandoning their property rights. As for the case of Tian's supplementary prices, which was intended to pay for the land that people initially received, they were only required to pay for the beach. Once the land was enclosed and cultivated into fields, the income was abundant and the profits were high. Accordingly, the price of the field should be paid separately and be graded and taxed in accordance with the regulations. An announcement was issued previously urging each of the property owners in the case. Now it has been investigated that the case documents show that very few of the property owners have followed the rules to report and receive the supplementary price, while there are still many who deliberately conceal and delay, the reasons being to tidy up the old cases, rectify the national debts, and increase tax revenues. It is not convenient to let it drag on any longer. In addition to the county government strictly urging the reporting to receive and pay the price within a time limit, the announcement to each of the property owners will now be issued to inform all parties. All official Hamadi land, the original new accretion, and the enclosed and reclaimed Tian lands etc. must, from the date of this notice, come to the Bureau within one month to comply with the regulations for reporting, receiving the supplementary price, and grading the taxes. If there is a further overdue report in an attempt to resist, then, once it is discovered or reported, the punishment will be halved in accordance with the regulations. The matter concerns the interests of each of the property owners and should not be viewed as a mere formality, leading to self-misfortune.

The Executive Yuan submitted the proposal to the 42nd meeting of the Executive Yuan for resolution. After receiving this official document, the charitable organizations believed that tens of millions of disaster victims across the country are now clamoring for relief. If an additional burden of 2.3 million yuan is added to the railway relief transportation each year, even if it is taken directly from the relief funds, it is indirectly taken from the disaster victims. It is heard that they are uniting various charitable organizations to send a telegram to the Executive Yuan, requesting that it withdraw the order.

Business News - Financial - Gold Market Weekly: Reaction After Five Consecutive Weeks of Rise; Unified Assessment Drops Thirteen Taels and Three Mace

Over the past week, the standard gold price has been in a state of near fluctuation, unpredictable. Daily differences have exceeded ten taels, leaving people in a fog. The demands of various firms have varied, and intentions have been complex, ultimately leading to decline. The August opening at the beginning of the week was relatively stable, dropping only four mace, to 761 taels. As the silver market continued to rise, drafts in this city also extended, but by Tuesday, it had suddenly broken through 750 taels, abruptly reaching 47.5 taels. Subsequently, the silver market seemed to contract, trending upwards. The highest price on Wednesday was 64 taels, but the situation was uncertain, fluctuating around 60 taels. Afterward, due to rollover considerations, there were many short positions. Although spot goods have seemed to increase recently, they ultimately needed to be covered, so they urgently advanced, returning to favorable conditions. By the weekend, there was a sudden shift to weakness. Unexpectedly, the Bank of England reported a rising trend again, and the London market seemed to have a bullish outlook. It had already re-entered 50 taels, and then closed at 48 taels and one mace. The total weekly difference was 16 taels and five mace, and the unified assessment fell by 13 taels and three mace compared to the previous Saturday, a reversal after five consecutive weeks of rise. However, Saturday happened to be the 16th, marking the beginning of the rollover, with September entering the market. The opening was 748 taels and five mace, and the closing was 45 taels and one mace, causing the short positions to cover 5.78 to 3 taels, but there was no excessive complexity. The positions of various firms, both long and short, were recorded in yesterday's report. The British and American silver markets have been rising for three consecutive weeks. The Shanghai British exchange rate rose by 1.5 increments (375), and the American exchange rate rose by only 25. The domestic market also tended towards relaxation. Sterling continued to rise by 375, exceeding eight pence, while the US dollar rose by only 31.25, actually due to smaller exchange rate reversals. Gold dealers and speculators were scrambling, and market conditions changed daily. The unified assessment of the British-US exchange rate fell by 3.75, and the US-British exchange rate also fell by 2.8125, while the settlement price was calculated around 70 taels in US dollars. Again, based on the transaction price of the day, the hedge was 30+ taels away (forward US dollar). The naked spot price was from 7 taels 7 mace 5 candareens to 7 taels. Finally, due to the rollover, it should be incrementally increased to 9 taels 7 mace 5 candareens. I will now extract the general overview of the week below.

Weekly Overview:

Monday:

Large silver rose again by 1875 to 125. US silver continued by 125. Sterling and the US dollar did not move. The internal market tended to harden. Dealers initially bought and then sold. The standard gold price for August opened at 761 taels, down only four candareens, because US silver rose but was short. Subsequently, it increased to 63 taels and eight mace. Afterward, sellers showed bravery, and the exchange market loosened, breaking through 60 taels. At noon, it was 56 taels and eight mace, and the closing was 58 taels and four mace. The afternoon opened at 58 taels and eight mace. Then, large holders sold off, dropping to the 50 tael mark, then to 53 taels and eight mace. By the closing, it was 3 taels and three mace, falling by 8 taels and one mace compared to the previous Saturday, the fourth day of slight decline. The highest price of the day was 63 taels and eight mace, and the lowest price was 50 taels, a difference of 13 taels and eight mace. The fluctuations were significant, and the settlements were complex.

Tuesday:

The rising trend of large silver had not yet ended. It increased by 125 to 1875. US silver increased by 25, and Sterling lengthened by 25. The US dollar also only increased by 25, which was a small exchange rate squeeze. The internal market tended to be different, loosening and then tightening. The gold market initially opened at 755 taels, rising by 1 tael and seven candareens, because the exchange rate had violently fallen. The private telegram silver price also increased by 25, especially as sellers drummed up the exchange rate, which loosened and flooded, falling sharply, breaking through 50 taels, finally reaching 47.5 taels. Then, various firms enthusiastically pursued, and the exchange market rebounded, the price flourished, soaring by more than 10 taels, reaching 58 taels and eight mace. The noon closing was 6 taels and two candareens, and the afternoon was 6 taels seven candareens to 7 taels five candareens. Later, because there seemed to be many sellers, it retreated to 54 taels and two candareens, suddenly jumping up 4 taels, reaching 58 taels and five mace. The highest price of the day was 58 taels and eight mace, and the lowest was 47 taels and five mace, a difference of 11 taels and three mace. Securities: Last Week's Bond Prices Fluctuated Slightly Higher

Trends Mixed, with Over 20 Million Transacted

Last week (from July 11th to 16th), the transactions of spot and futures at the local Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange were as follows: The inflow and outflow of spot financial assets fluctuated sharply, while other transactions remained scarce. The total weekly transaction volume was 600,100 yuan, of which financial assets accounted for 500,000 yuan, 194,700 yuan for unified assets, 26,000 yuan for customs duties, 10,000 yuan for 19 bonds, and only a few thousand yuan for the remainder. 96 bonds have not been issued. In the futures market, price fluctuations were relatively large, and market sentiment was slightly more active. Moreover, the August futures market gradually became active, so the transaction volume far exceeded the previous period. The total transaction volume for the week was 19,575,000 yuan. Unified taxes accounted for a larger portion, with 3.14 million yuan for July and 1.12 million yuan for August. Unified taxes accounted for 2.36 million yuan for July and 765,000 yuan for August. 20 customs bonds accounted for 1.985 million yuan for July and 645,000 yuan for August. 20 cigarette bonds accounted for 1.995 million yuan for July and 685,000 yuan for August. 19 charity bonds accounted for 2.005 million yuan for July and 145,000 yuan for August. Reorganization bonds accounted for a total of 640,000 yuan, and customs duties accounted for 420,000 yuan. The current month of issued "Whole 6" bonds accounted for only 150,000 yuan, and only 75,000 yuan for "Nine Six" bonds. There was also no market for the August issues. As for the trend of bond prices during the week, they were more active than the previous week. The first day of the week was the most sluggish, with supply and demand both clear, and minimal changes. On Tuesday and Wednesday, market sentiment suddenly became optimistic, and investment and inflows were quite active. Buying sentiment surpassed selling, and prices rose uniformly, with daily rebounds ranging from 45 cents to over 1 yuan. Thursday was quiet, with prices rising before falling. On Friday, as the situation showed little progress, prices fell back by around 56 cents. On the last day of the weekend, market sentiment was dull, with minimal fluctuations. Judging from the situation, it seemed that it would gradually become calm and difficult to develop for the time being. As a result, it rebounded slightly compared to the previous week. Except for the 20 cigarette bonds and spot unified taxes, which had no market on the weekend, each rose by 1 yuan and 20 cents. The others improved by 12 cents to around 78 cents. Grain: The River Rice Market Fell and Then Hardened

South Shanghai:

Yesterday, the rice market saw a relatively scarce supply from various gangs, arriving at about five or six firms. Stocks were not weak. City and rural shop sales have long been bottoming out. Since the Japanese Incident, customers have raised prices, causing people to become depressed. Transactions were slightly more numerous. Thick japonica rice immediately rose by 2 jiao. The rural village gang slightly moved, with opening fluctuations of 3 jiao. Although the quantity of clear ocean pointed goods was scattered, sales were sluggish, and market prices temporarily followed the original level.

New Gate:

Yesterday, there were some arrivals, about fourteen or fifteen firms. Those approaching the market in the morning were not enthusiastic. Thick japonica top goods were particularly stable. The mid-range shop appetite gradually moved, and prices slightly rose. Thin indica arrivals and sales were even, and the situation continued to strengthen. Early rice was intermittent, with no standard, because stock arrivals were low, and buyers were not paying attention. Prices were stable. The transformation of Yin yuan wine households still had strong demand, and market prices rose by about 1 jiao.

Silk and Tea: Last Week's Silk Market Became Even More Lifeless

Japanese silk is aggressively selling into the mainland...Factory silk sales to Japan are trending sluggish...European and American silk factories are reducing work during summer vacation...Raw silk consumption is greatly reduced...

During the middle of last week, the local foreign firm silk market became even more lifeless, with barely any market activity to record. Japanese silk is actively dumping its products, which is the biggest reason why the sales of Chinese silk are becoming increasingly sluggish. European and American markets are flooded with Japanese silk. Silk weaving factories are all reducing work and stopping machines during the summer vacation. The inquiries for Chinese silk telegraphed in from Europe and America are very rare. Recently, white factory silk has been entirely reliant on the demand from mainland silk merchants, and transactions are still not deserted. Unexpectedly, lately, Japanese silk has been encroaching on mainland sales, greatly affecting the sales of silk from domestic users. Last week's transactions suddenly became sparse, and prices also plummeted by dozens of taels. Market sentiment became increasingly sluggish. European and American Chinese silk markets almost had transactions without trade. The Finale of the Wutun Tea Market

Wuyuan:

Local tea firms did not dare to increase production to the fullest extent because the Shanghai market was sluggish and prices were low. Those who were cautious mainly focused on completing one batch of tea and closing the market. In the past ten days, about fifty companies in various villages have completed production and closed the market. There are also companies with more daring, who are continuing to purchase local mountain household goods because current mountain prices are low and the Russian Estate Cooperative will soon begin operations, and tea sales are gradually turning around. Therefore, in recent days, there have been more instances of opening scales and conducting transactions. Prices range from 42 yuan to 50 yuan, which is 20 yuan lower per dan than the initial market price.

Tunxi:

In the Tunxi market, sales of rare needle embroidery tribute grades of boxed tea transported to Shanghai by various firms have gradually started in the past ten days. Except for the fact that rare market prices are difficult to increase, the rest are similar to last year. The concerns of the firms about tea sales being stagnant have now been slightly alleviated. However, the influx of tea to the source is still surging. According to a recent survey, there is a huge stockpile of more than 6,000 dan. If the Shanghai market becomes popular from now on, the appetite of each firm will still be quite substantial, so the tea hawkers are actually more anxious than the tea firms. The shop and estate tea bandits, who once sold well for a time, have recently seen their market prices fall to 20 yuan due to full stomachs and fine sales, 16 yuan lower per dan than before. Those who generally collected tea bandits have stopped operations because of this.

Report on Comfort Money

The 19th Route Army's heroic resistance against Japan in Shanghai has been recognized worldwide, and there is no need for further praise. Yesterday, the General Headquarters of the 19th Route Army sent the first report on the receipt of comfort money for the anti-Japanese war, and I cannot help but make some expectations on this point.

It is a common thing for people from all walks of life to comfort the 19th Route Army, and for the 19th Route Army to report the total amount of income and expenditure to the public after receiving the comfort money. However, in the current military and political organs, such bright and upright actions are rare.

Our newspaper receives work reports from various provinces and agencies every day. Opening them up, we see that they are mostly grand and ornate articles. The result is nothing more than self-promotion, vigorously touting themselves in every possible way, which is meaningless. When the 19th Route Army was bravely fighting the enemy in Shanghai, people from all agencies were angered by the enemy's aggression, and everyone's blood boiled, generously donating money to comfort the soldiers. The people were just doing their part to serve the country, and did not care about the amount of income and how it was distributed.

The first report of the 19th Route Army reported the total amount of comfort money received in detail to the public, and the report on the use of comfort money stated that how it was distributed was temporarily kept secret due to military secrets, and would be announced to China and foreign countries immediately at the appropriate time to show credibility. What a bright and upright action this is.

The hard-earned money of our people is paid to officials every year in the form of donations, taxes, and public bonds, etc., but we have never seen officials take such beautiful actions, reporting a detailed account to the people. Although the people of our country only have the obligation to pay taxes and no right to supervise the use of funds, in their hearts, they always feel a little uncomfortable and unhappy.

Science: The Method of Making Nitric Acid - Dream

As for China's acid industry, it is still in its infancy. There are only one or two manufacturing plants in the country, and they are small in scale and outdated in methods. They are mostly attached to military factories, so their output is only enough to supply the military factories, let alone industrial and agricultural industries. Now, the Ministry of Industry is planning to sign a contract with Germany to jointly build a large-scale manufacturing plant in Pukou to supply national defense industries. This is a very good intention. Among the important acids, the methods of making hydrochloric acid and sulfuric acid have already been published in this journal one after another, so now we should sequentially describe the method of making nitric acid.

The Method of Making Nitric Acid Using Saltpeter

This method is used in industry and in the laboratory. However, since the invention of the new method, this method has gradually been eliminated in industry. The method is to mix nitrate and acid, and nitric acid is formed by chemical reaction. Commonly used nitrate is sodium nitrate, and the acid is sulfuric acid, because it is cheap.

The Method of Using Nitrogen in the Air

Although there is a lot of nitrogen in the air, it is extremely difficult for humans to combine it with oxygen, except for a small portion of plants that can directly use it. Even at a high temperature of 3,000 degrees, the amount of nitrogen combined with oxygen only accounts for 5%. However, since the invention of the use of electricity, countries with extremely cheap electricity prices, such as Sweden and Norway, have all adopted this method. The method is to introduce air into the two poles of the discharge, and part of the air becomes nitrous oxide. Then the temperature is lowered to about 400 or 500 degrees, and the nitrous oxide is combined with the air to form nitrogen dioxide. This purple-yellow gas becomes commonly used nitric acid after being absorbed by water.

The Method of Manufacturing by Platinum

During the European War, Germany used it most frequently. 精 gas is mixed with air and passed through a platinum plate catalyst, and dilute nitric acid is formed by gasification. However, the gas must be clean when passing through, otherwise, it will be very harmful to the catalyst.

Nitric acid is a very strong acid and is rich in oxidizing properties. It is very easy to catch fire and can be used to make powerful explosives and smokeless gunpowder. If it is combined with lime, it becomes fertilizer. Other things such as artificial ivory and artificial pigments cannot do without it.

Italian Army to Hold Regular Large-Scale Maneuvers 54

Starting on the 21st of this month, continuing for approximately two weeks.

Applying mechanical exercises as much as possible to practice mobile warfare.

Participating military strength: 50,000 men.

Havas, Rome, 16th - The Italian Army's large-scale maneuvers are scheduled to begin on the 21st of this month and continue until August 6th. General Garrazzo is the commander-in-chief. General Garrazzo has never approved of siege warfare during the European War, and adheres to the doctrine of mobile warfare. During this exercise, various mechanical methods will be applied as much as possible, and the situation will be extremely impressive. The total military strength participating in the exercise is 50,000 men, including 20,000 reservists, which is a significant increase compared to last year.

Hyogo Prefecture, Japan Holds Air Defense Drill 57

Rengo News Agency, Kobe, 17th - This morning at 10:00 AM, sixteen villages in Hyogo Prefecture held Japan's first civilian air defense drill. Participating troops included the 3rd, 4th, and 16th Divisions, the Army Flying School in Akeno, civilian troops, veterans, youth groups, women's associations, maiden associations, and other group members, totaling 40,000 people. Organized into water defense, rescue, and fire-fighting squads, they began their activities. Japan, Impoverished by Militarism 58

Falling into Financial Straits

The Japanese Minister of Finance Lamented This.

Havas, Tokyo Correspondence, 16th - When someone asked the Minister of Finance for his opinion on the falling price of Japanese gold, the Minister replied as follows: "Since the beginning of Japanese history, it has never experienced such difficult times. Whether looking at the financial problem, the relief of farmers, or the Manchurian problem, each alone constitutes an extremely serious problem. Some say that Japan is currently engaged in a major battle involving life and death, and this is no exaggeration. However, the Japanese people do not seem to fully understand this serious situation. In Britain or the United States, the government can increase taxes, reduce spending, or attempt to reduce the military. Why are these methods feasible in countries like Britain and the United States? Because their people can cooperate with the government. What about Japan? Our neighbors, the Chinese and the Russians, are forcing us to use troops. We have no choice but to maintain our military, so that there is no room for savings in the military. Judging from the current situation, it is necessary to issue patriotic bonds. However, to prevent an emergency against foreign powers, we are particularly unwilling to use up part of our existing financial resources again, especially since our existing financial resources are not sufficient in the first place. As for increasing taxes, it only makes up for the budget deficit, which is not very helpful. Moreover, even if we intend to increase taxes, it is impossible given the current situation. Considering the situation of the Japanese state, there can be no optimism. The longer the term of bonds issued abroad, the lower their value, which shows that foreign countries hold a pessimistic view of Japan's future. The continued fall of the Japanese yen is due to the reduction of our country's real economic power, so I have no way to prevent it from falling further. Any attempt to rescue the currency price by unnatural methods will ultimately be in vain, and will instead give speculators new data. Therefore, at present, there is no other way but to let it take its natural course. Speaking of this, I am truly heartbroken, but there is nothing I can do. I am extremely concerned about the future of Japan. My only hope is that things will turn around after reaching an extreme, and that there will be a turning point after exhaustion."

Northeast Administrative Unification Issue 59

Japanese Military Demands Revision of Director-General Title

New Wine in Old Bottles

Rengo, Tokyo, 17th - The Army authorities, as a result of extremely important and careful consideration of the problem of unifying the four-headed politics of Manchuria, have decided to revise the original plan. Minister of the Army Araki submitted his revised plan to the Prime Minister and Foreign Minister after yesterday's cabinet meeting, requesting consideration. The points that have been revised are as follows: (1) The Director-General system may cause misunderstandings of interfering in Manchurian politics, so it is changed to the Manchurian Special Envoy Plenipotentiary Office. (2) Therefore, the Special Envoy Director-General is changed to the Special Envoy Plenipotentiary, and the Deputy Director-General is changed to the Secretary-General. As for the Financial and Colonial Industries Bureaus, they are not actually necessary, and are changed to the Internal Affairs and Criminal Affairs Bureaus. Japanese councilors are dispatched to the Manchurian State Council to guide the administrative affairs of Manchuria.

There, at the Institute of Balneotherapeutics attached to Kyushu University, he will strive to recover from his illness and at the same time practice walking with his artificial leg.
